<userid>106538710158412913945</userid><Name>C Lee</Name><Date>1593605832800<//Date><Rate>5</Rate>< text>
Hidden gem in the area. I heard it get busy for dinner so we came right when they opened on a Saturday, we got seated right away. The staff and the owners were very delightful and generous!

We got the Omakase and the clam dish for starters with two bottles of sake. All the sashimi was fresh and high quality. Yuzu cheesecake and green tea ice cream were good. I enjoyed the intimate vibe here. We had such a great time with our friends.</text>

<rate>5<//rate><Text>Came around 7pm, didn't have to wait to get a seat. Most of the fish and sashimi are of good quality, a plus. We sat at the bar and observed that the chef was considerate enough to let the sliced fish to cool down to rice temperature before serving them as nigiri. I got the sashimi omakaze($20 for 5 piece) and my girlfriend got the nigiri omakaze ($40 for 8 pieces). After the first round, confirmed that the food here are worth a stop, I continued to my second round of ordering. Chi and oo toro ($7 and $9 per piece) nigiri: good. Then I ordered a nigiri dinner, 6 pieces with miso soup ($36): above satisfactory.</Text>< Pics>

< Text>
Has really good deals for odds and ends that would normally cost at least a few bucks elsewhere.  Even better deals than the wish app.  Sometimes there are long lines and the parking lot can be crazy, and shopping carts can sometimes be less accessible when they get left outside, so I prefer to go in the mornings during the week when things are calmer and it is easier to take my time and see what good deals they have in stock.  Stock changes often.  I recommend this place for organization type stuff, school supplies, party stuff, gift bags, greeting cards, and basic kitchen utensils.  Definitely the place to go if shopping for a college dorm or apartment.</Text>

<rating>5< /rating><text>We have been thinking about getting a futon couch for accommodating guest from out of town. I was not sure what the cost would be as I have never gotten one. When we went to the store Sheng was with another customer but greeted us and asked us what we were looking for. When I saw the price tag I was  surprised to see the prices as I they were more expensive than I thought they would be. However, it was Memorial Day weekend and they had very good sales. The organic mattresses looked attractive but they were quite expensive so we went with the standard one.

There are less expensive futon beds out there but the frames are flimsy and the mattresses are not as comfortable. The whole idea of us getting a futon bed is that when guests come over they don't have to sleep on a blow up bed and be comfortable. You get what you pay for.

The wooden frame looks very sturdy and easy to pull out. We had three different choices on color for the frame and we got the black walnut. All of their mattresses and covers are made to order (in SF) so keep in mind there could be 2 to 3 week lead time. It is quite impressive the different fabrics and color you get to choose from for the cover.

We got the standard mattress type and the medium level collection. Sheng helped us pick the right mattress based on the usage. Since they make their own mattresses if your mattress goes bad you can replace it. They do have a 7-year limited warranty though. Or if you want to change the color of the cover you can always purchase a new one.
We had picked a very light cream color but Sheng was kind enough to suggest a darker tint and we got the khaki.

He also mentioned that we should get the rubber pad as you will need it to stop the mattress from slipping. He was very honest with us and said that we can get it for cheaper at Walmart next door as all you have to do is cut it to size. We appreciated the fact that he was straightforward with us but for the price difference, time and effort, it just made sense to get it from them.

The delivery is $70 and only $40 for assembly. We got a queen size futon bed for $1158 including delivery and assembly. Since they have the bed frame in stock, we are getting the futon bed in less than a week. I highly recommend shopping at the Futon Shop if you are looking for quality futon beds.<//text><Pics>None<//Pics>< response>

<rate>5</rate>< Text>
I bought my FR-S in 2013 and at the time the dealership had licenses plates sent directly to them to be then then handed to me. During my first scheduled maintenance they felt compelled to "Help me out" and installed the front license plate mount which required 2 sizeable holes to be drilled into the front bumper (painted).  They didn't realize that I had (in the trunk) a specialty relocator and would never want to drill holes in the front of my car! (Who would do this to an FR-S?!)

Of course the dealership felt it wasn't an issue which they could resolve, citing legal requirements to install the plates. A few months later for my birthday my wife decided to cover the cost to have it repaired. I went to approximately 5 Collision repair shops, every one of them advised that the cost of repair would be $1000 or more and take up to 5 days. They indicated repainting the entire front of the car including the hood was needed.

A friend recommended Bumper DOC for a repair as he got repair done for less than half the price of quoted collision shops. He said the process was easy and the owners work with customers directly so you don't feel like just an ATM machine. At the time this specific shop (in Santee) was unknown to me so I tried the Kearny Mesa shop first. Got a quote and met the owner in the process. I was blown away when he explained it would take 1 day and cost $350, but of course ! was more than a little skeptical so I sat on it for a few weeks, at which point I decided to pull the trigger. By this point I had found out about the Santee location so I brought it in and met Buddy, this guy was just as Friendly, polite and professional as the owner of Kearny Mesa. Before I even had a chance to explain that I had already got a quote he said it would be $350 and take a Day or less to do, of course my wife paid them and the work was done.

I was shocked by the result, it was a flawless execution, the paint match was spectacular, there were no issues and event put on a custom emblem to replace the stock one for me.This was finished on January 21st of 2014.

Flash Forward to March 23rd 2015 (more than 14 months later), I have always been religious about washing my car by hand, I hate  carwashes and avoid them at all costs. This car is a bit more than a daily driver, its a Street Modified Class SCCA Car which I race around in Southern California venues. The day of a large national event the car was filthy, I hadn't driven it in a few weeks and that night would be required to put a bunch of sponsorship decals on the paint, so I decided to drive through a new touchless wash about 4 blocks from Bumper Doc. The car wash seemed to go fine until I walked around to wipe off the excess water and noticed that a huge chunk of paint was blasted off the front-end. I panicked a bit and drove directly over to show Buddy, not even remembering who I was told me it was covered if he could just have the car for a few days. So about 2 weeks later I brought the car in and left it for 7 days (more than he needed but in my eyes didn't want to inconvenience him), not only did he fix the car, he hand washed it and fixed a dent in the lower splitter (definitely was my fault). BumperDOC and owners like Buddy are a rare breed of service related businesses who care more about customer satisfaction than the bottom line. Not only will he get my business forever, I will make sure I recommend his shop to every person in need of his type of help.

Thanks guys!!<//Text>

<user>113855869943630789040< /user><Name>Geydi Valenzuela<//Name><Date>1478844429213< /Date>< Rate>

< Text>
**From my Yelp Review**

Who knew learning about the health of your peepers could be fun?

Dr. Steensma reminds me of Dr. Oz; they make learning about your health exciting. He exudes genuine passion about his profession as well as shows true concern for your eye health.

If you can, get the CT scan for your eyes (about $30 I believe).
It was so much fun to see my eyeballs, haha. It's neat to actually see all the veins and arteries that connect to it in a 3D-like format. Thanks to all the machines and technology that was used, I feel at peace about the health of my eyes.

I didn't end up buying contacts since unfortunately my eyes are extremely dry at the moment (we're working on it) so I can't comment on the brands they offer or their prices. The glasses though, are on point. They offer the ever classic Ray Bans, Kate Spade, Coach and more! Their prices are fair and the lens warranty is even better, two years if I recall correctly? (dont quote me) I believe they also advised that if my lenses were to get scratched within the first year they could smoth the scratches out for me.

The service I received from Dr. Steensma and the lovely ladies that make up his staff was amazing; they are ready to answer any question you may have. I had a lot of fun (and no shame) taking selfies with some of the frames. The girl that assisted me (forgot to ask her name- Ooops!) was so patient and took out more frames for me to look at. Even though I took a while looking over their frame selection, I never felt pressured into buying them. In fact, Dr. Steenma had his staff correct my worn-out, low quality frames (bought them online for pennies- you get what you pay for) out of courtesy. No strings attached. That's quality service for ya!

Tip: They are ALWAYS booked so schedule in your appointment ahead of time. Totally worth the wait.

Ps I went to see another 'popular' Optometrist in the Ventura area prior to coming here and their service was very poor. Close to terrible actually.</Text>

< text>
Finally checking this place out! Always past the food truck and knew this was close by. Finally made it to the location! Right by the old farrell's ice cream parlor in small Shopping plaza, plenty of parking!

Limited Dining is allow, takeout, and delivery are other options as well. Large selection of tacos starting at $2.97, burritos, mulitas, Tortas, quesadilla, sopes, and various sides.

Went with lengua (it's tough to find), cabeza, and tripas (she offer to fried it and said it taste better as such). Pal went with pollo and al pastor and a side of rice. They ask if we wanted cilantro and onions on our tacos and we opted  for them.

2 corn tortillas Street taco style with our choice but was missing cilantro and onion but came with red and green salsa and lime wedges.

Meat was very tender. Fried tripas was crunchy and did not taste heavy nor was it overly greasy. Cabeza and lengua was soft, easy to chew, melt in your mouth.

If your looking for alcohol, they do not serve any here.

Service was friendly and great to support another local business! Definitely will return!</text>

<text>I'm always up for a new place especially if the focus is on the food. This makes it convenient if the place is small because the food can be taken out and enjoyed without losing the feel of the place.
That is important here because it is smaller and could be crowded easily.

The variety is small but that is not necessarily a negative.  That means they combine what they have without going outside the core which in this case  is the meats.

The meats are well prepared,  and do not need a lot of sauces or additions to make them satisfying. There is a area for sauces that can help but not necessary with the basic taco or burrito.

The main drawback here is the beans, I am kinda judgy about the refried beans and here they dont cut it. Bland and just filler. The other thing is the staff did not seems enthused to be there. So why should I be?

So, grab some tacos,  skip the beans and take it to go.

As always I say, try different things here for yourself, they have lengua, cabeza  and other meats to try, and judge for yourself.</text><pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipN8PrRHDLtMEzafApmbG7i1di21G6TXjeXxy4cT=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNk125Vz8n2V-Z1_ZXP9eukGmMlTHHaPpdzYiLy=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMscmTtFd4YwfeX-lMInmdtyD5loOX92uYRkxra=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMEdy2tBDNgsKm-z3NLxMcmruJ0gesqJmdIPS-I=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMilBndB3oxCsAPq77KiobAJXcbODVcLC9V2qci=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOjpadb9UgdBtftjXPWn5OrPTi0v7uTEA2CB8VH=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]</pictures>< resp>
